  471. Let me start by saying, as someone that suffers from Trichotillomania and has to wear a wig daily, high quality is of the utmost importance to me. This sentiment rings especially true after receiving this wig.<br /><br />I was hesitant to purchase a wig online because I'm really picky and what a wig looks like on a stand isn't always what it looks like on your head. I'm glad the reviewer didn't have any negative effects but typically heat melts synthetic hair. Even heat from opening the oven can melt the hair.<br /><br />Back to my review: If you're looking for an affordable and realistic looking wig I definitely recommend this one!
